- **keps/993-two-phase-admission/README.md:169** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-08-23T15:37:29Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,280 @@
+# KEP-993: Two Stage Admission Process
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories (Optional)](#user-stories-optional)
+    - [Story 1](#story-1)
+    - [Story 2](#story-2)
+  - [Notes/Constraints/Caveats (Optional)](#notesconstraintscaveats-optional)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+      - [Prerequisite testing updates](#prerequisite-testing-updates)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+This KEP defines the extension point to plug in arbitrary, additional checks
+for workloads before they are admitted for execution. These external checks may
+be implemented inside or outside of Kueue and may provide functionality like
+budgeting, capacity provisioning or some elements of multicluster dispatching.
+
+## Motivation
+
+With the growth of Kueue, not all desired elements may land inside of the core
+Kueue. Some users may even not want to publish their custom admission logic in
+a public repository. At the same time, we don’t want to force users to
+fork Kueue. Thus, an pluggable mechanism for workload admission needs to
+be established.
+
+### Goals
+
+Define mechanism to allow external controllers:
+
+* to give green light to admit a workload.
+* to temporarily hold workload admission.
+* to stop a previously admitted workload and move it back to the
+suspended state.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Provide a specific design or implementation for any external controller.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Extend ClusterQueue definition with a list of external controller names that
+need to give green light to admit a workload. Until all of the controllers, which
+identify with these names, don’t give a green light, the workload will not
+be admitted. 
+
+Each workload that goes to such a queue, will get additional conditions, 
+in a dedicated field in the status, each reflecting the go/no-go 
+decision of each of the external controllers. Once
+a controller is confident that the workload can be admitted, it flips the
+status of the corresponding condition from "Unknown" to "True". 
+
+If a controller changes its mind about a workload, it can switch the condition
+back to false and the workload will be immediately suspended.
+
+### User Stories (Optional)
+
+#### Story 1
+
+I want to use the [Cluster Autoscaler ProvisioningRequest API](https://github.com/kubernetes/autoscaler/pull/5848) 
+to ensure that the resources can be provided in full before starting the workload.  
+
+#### Story 2
+
+I want to base workload admission on budget. I have the actual consumption metrics
+in my Prometheus/Datadog/Stackdriver/whatever monitoring system. And weekly
+budget in a CRD, per namespace. I’m happy to modify some small existing sample
+controller, but I don’t want to fork the whole Kueue to adjust some minor details.
+ 
+### Notes/Constraints/Caveats (Optional)
+
+Each of the go/no-go decisions is best-effort and can be reversed at any time. 
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+## Design Details
+
+TL;DR; 
+* extend ClusterQueueSpec with the list of checks.
+* add extra conditions to Workload status.
+* introduce new CRD, AdmissionCheck.
+
+Details:
+
+We will extend ClusterQueueSpec definition by adding a reference to
+AdmissionChecks that the queue needs to perform before admitting a
+workload. The design of AdmissionChecks is similar to IngressClass
+- it allows passing additional parameters, specific to particular checks
+that need to be performed. 
+
+```
+// ClusterQueueSpec defines the desired state of ClusterQueue.
+type ClusterQueueSpec struct {
+[...]
+	// List of AdmissionCheck names that needs to be passed
+	// to admit a workload. The order of the checks doesn't matter,
+	// all of them will be started at the same time.
+	AdmissionChecks []string `json:"admissionChecks"`
+}
+
+// WorkloadStatus defines the observed state of Workload.
+type WorkloadStatus struct {
+[...]
+	// Status of admission checks, if there are any specified 
+	// for the ClusterQueue in which the workload is queued.
+	AdmissionChecksConditions []metav1.Condition `json:"admissionChecksConditions,omitempty"`
+}
+
+// Condition names used in WorkloadStatus
+const (
+	AdmissionPrecheck string = "AdmissionPrecheck"
+)
+
+// Cluster-scoped top-level object defining a check that 
+// can be referenced in ClusterQueue.
+type AdmissionCheck struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta   `json:",inline"`
+	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
+	Spec AdmissionCheckSpec `json:"spec,omitempty"`
+}
+
+// Condition Reasons used by AdmissionChecks.
+const (
+	// The check cannot pass at this moment, back off (possibly 
+	// allowing other to try, unblock quota) and retry. Can be set only
+	// when Condition status is set to "False"
+	Retry string = "Retry"
+	// The check will not pass in the near future. It is not worth
+	// to retry. Can be set together with Condition status "False".
+	Reject string = "Reject"
+	// The check might pass if there was fewer workloads. Proceed
+	// with any pending workload preemption. Should be set 
+	// when condition status is still "Unknown" 
+	BookQuotaRequired status = "BookQuotaRequired"
+)
+
+// AdmissionCheckSpec defines the desired state of AdmissionCheck.
+type AdmissionCheckSpec struct {
+	// Name of the controller which will actually perform
+	// the checks. This is the name with which controller indentifies with,
+	// not a K8S pod or deployment name. Cannot be empty. 
+	ControllerName string `json:"controllerName"`
+
+	// How long to keep the workload suspended 
+	// after a failed check (after it transitioned to False).
+	// After that the check state goes to "Unknown".
+	// The default is 15 min. 
+	RetryDelayMinutes *int64 `json:"retryDelayMinutes,omitempty"`
+
+	// A reference to the additional parameters for the check. 
+	Parameters *AdmissionCheckParametersReference `json:"parameters,omitempty"`
+
+	// How should the workload book quota (and possibly preempt others) 
+	// before the check pass. The default is NoBooking.
+	// If different modes are used for different AdmissionChecks,
+	// the most restrictive one is used.
```

  Can you list them here in order of restrictiveness? IIUC, BookAfterQuotaCheck is more restrictive.

- **keps/993-two-phase-admission/README.md:181** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-08-23T15:39:56Z

+## Summary

+for workloads before they are admitted for execution. These external checks may

+budgeting, capacity provisioning or some elements of multicluster dispatching.
+
+## Motivation
+
+With the growth of Kueue, not all desired elements may land inside of the core
+Kueue. Some users may even not want to publish their custom admission logic in
+a public repository. At the same time, we don’t want to force users to
+fork Kueue. Thus, an pluggable mechanism for workload admission needs to
+be established.
+
+### Goals
+
+Define mechanism to allow external controllers:
+
+* to give green light to admit a workload.
+* to temporarily hold workload admission.
+* to stop a previously admitted workload and move it back to the
+suspended state.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Provide a specific design or implementation for any external controller.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Extend ClusterQueue definition with a list of external controller names that
+need to give green light to admit a workload. Until all of the controllers, which
+identify with these names, don’t give a green light, the workload will not
+be admitted. 
+
+Each workload that goes to such a queue, will get additional conditions, 
+in a dedicated field in the status, each reflecting the go/no-go 
+decision of each of the external controllers. Once
+a controller is confident that the workload can be admitted, it flips the
+status of the corresponding condition from "Unknown" to "True". 
+
+If a controller changes its mind about a workload, it can switch the condition
+back to false and the workload will be immediately suspended.
+
+### User Stories (Optional)
+
+#### Story 1
+
+I want to use the [Cluster Autoscaler ProvisioningRequest API](https://github.com/kubernetes/autoscaler/pull/5848) 
+to ensure that the resources can be provided in full before starting the workload.  
+
+#### Story 2
+
+I want to base workload admission on budget. I have the actual consumption metrics
+in my Prometheus/Datadog/Stackdriver/whatever monitoring system. And weekly
+budget in a CRD, per namespace. I’m happy to modify some small existing sample
+controller, but I don’t want to fork the whole Kueue to adjust some minor details.
+ 
+### Notes/Constraints/Caveats (Optional)
+
+Each of the go/no-go decisions is best-effort and can be reversed at any time. 
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+## Design Details
+
+TL;DR; 
+* extend ClusterQueueSpec with the list of checks.
+* add extra conditions to Workload status.
+* introduce new CRD, AdmissionCheck.
+
+Details:
+
+We will extend ClusterQueueSpec definition by adding a reference to
+AdmissionChecks that the queue needs to perform before admitting a
+workload. The design of AdmissionChecks is similar to IngressClass
+- it allows passing additional parameters, specific to particular checks
+that need to be performed. 
+
+```
+// ClusterQueueSpec defines the desired state of ClusterQueue.
+type ClusterQueueSpec struct {
+[...]
+	// List of AdmissionCheck names that needs to be passed
+	// to admit a workload. The order of the checks doesn't matter,
+	// all of them will be started at the same time.
+	AdmissionChecks []string `json:"admissionChecks"`
+}
+
+// WorkloadStatus defines the observed state of Workload.
+type WorkloadStatus struct {
+[...]
+	// Status of admission checks, if there are any specified 
+	// for the ClusterQueue in which the workload is queued.
+	AdmissionChecksConditions []metav1.Condition `json:"admissionChecksConditions,omitempty"`
+}
+
+// Condition names used in WorkloadStatus
+const (
+	AdmissionPrecheck string = "AdmissionPrecheck"
+)
+
+// Cluster-scoped top-level object defining a check that 
+// can be referenced in ClusterQueue.
+type AdmissionCheck struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta   `json:",inline"`
+	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
+	Spec AdmissionCheckSpec `json:"spec,omitempty"`
+}
+
+// Condition Reasons used by AdmissionChecks.
+const (
+	// The check cannot pass at this moment, back off (possibly 
+	// allowing other to try, unblock quota) and retry. Can be set only
+	// when Condition status is set to "False"
+	Retry string = "Retry"
+	// The check will not pass in the near future. It is not worth
+	// to retry. Can be set together with Condition status "False".
+	Reject string = "Reject"
+	// The check might pass if there was fewer workloads. Proceed
+	// with any pending workload preemption. Should be set 
+	// when condition status is still "Unknown" 
+	BookQuotaRequired status = "BookQuotaRequired"
+)
+
+// AdmissionCheckSpec defines the desired state of AdmissionCheck.
+type AdmissionCheckSpec struct {
+	// Name of the controller which will actually perform
+	// the checks. This is the name with which controller indentifies with,
+	// not a K8S pod or deployment name. Cannot be empty. 
+	ControllerName string `json:"controllerName"`
+
+	// How long to keep the workload suspended 
+	// after a failed check (after it transitioned to False).
+	// After that the check state goes to "Unknown".
+	// The default is 15 min. 
+	RetryDelayMinutes *int64 `json:"retryDelayMinutes,omitempty"`
+
+	// A reference to the additional parameters for the check. 
+	Parameters *AdmissionCheckParametersReference `json:"parameters,omitempty"`
+
+	// How should the workload book quota (and possibly preempt others) 
+	// before the check pass. The default is NoBooking.
+	// If different modes are used for different AdmissionChecks,
+	// the most restrictive one is used.
+	QuotaBooking *QuotaBookingMode `json:"quotaBooking,omitempty"`
+}
+
+const (
+	// No booking, unless a check explicitely asks for it reporting quota exhausted.
+	NoBooking QuotaBookingMode = "NoBooking"
+	
+	// Book quota (and preempt) immediately after the basic quota checks 
+	// are done, without waiting for the additional checks to cpmplete.
+	BookAfterQuotaCheck QuotaBookingMode = "BookAfterQuotaCheck"
```

  How about:
  - AfterAdmissionChecks
  - BeforeAdmissionChecks

- **keps/993-two-phase-admission/README.md:202** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-08-23T15:41:17Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,274 @@
+# KEP-993: Two Stage Admission Process
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories (Optional)](#user-stories-optional)
+    - [Story 1](#story-1)
+    - [Story 2](#story-2)
+  - [Notes/Constraints/Caveats (Optional)](#notesconstraintscaveats-optional)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+      - [Prerequisite testing updates](#prerequisite-testing-updates)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+This KEP defines the extension point to plug in arbitrary, additional checks
+for workloads before they are admitted for execution. These external checks may
+be implemented inside or outside of Kueue and may provide functionality like
+budgeting, capacity provisioning or some elements of multicluster dispatching.
+
+## Motivation
+
+With the growth of Kueue, not all desired elements may land inside of the core
+Kueue. Some users may even not want to publish their custom admission logic in
+a public repository. At the same time, we don’t want to force users to
+fork Kueue. Thus, an pluggable mechanism for workload admission needs to
+be established.
+
+### Goals
+
+Define mechanism to allow external controllers:
+
+* to give green light to admit a workload.
+* to temporarily hold workload admission.
+* to stop a previously admitted workload and move it back to the
+suspended state.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Provide a specific design or implementation for any external controller.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Extend ClusterQueue definition with a list of external controller names that
+need to give green light to admit a workload. Until all of the controllers, which
+identify with these names, don’t give a green light, the workload will not
+be admitted. 
+
+Each workload that goes to such a queue, will get additional conditions, 
+in a dedicated field in the status, each reflecting the go/no-go 
+decision of each of the external controllers. Once
+a controller is confident that the workload can be admitted, it flips the
+status of the corresponding condition from false to true. 
+
+If a controller changes its mind about a workload, it can switch the condition
+back to false and the workload will be immediately suspended.
+
+### User Stories (Optional)
+
+#### Story 1
+
+I want to use the [Cluster Autoscaler ProvisioningRequest API](https://github.com/kubernetes/autoscaler/pull/5848) 
+to ensure that the resources can be provided in full before starting the workload.  
+
+#### Story 2
+
+I want to base workload admission on budget. I have the actual consumption metrics
+in my Prometheus/Datadog/Stackdriver/whatever monitoring system. And weekly
+budget in a CRD, per namespace. I’m happy to modify some small existing sample
+controller, but I don’t want to fork the whole Kueue to adjust some minor details.
+ 
+### Notes/Constraints/Caveats (Optional)
+
+Each of the go/no-go decisions is best-effort and can be reversed at any time. 
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+## Design Details
+
+TL;DR; 
+* extend ClusterQueueSpec with the list of checks.
+* add extra conditions to Workload status.
+* introduce new CRD, AdmissionCheck.
+
+Details:
+
+We will extend ClusterQueueSpec definition by adding a reference to
+AdmissionChecks that the queue needs to perform before admitting a
+workload. The design of AdmissionChecks is similar to IngressClass
+- it allows passing additional parameters, specific to particular checks
+that need to be performed. 
+
+```
+// ClusterQueueSpec defines the desired state of ClusterQueue
+type ClusterQueueSpec struct {
+[...]
+	// List of AdmissionCheck names that needs to be passed
+	// to admit a workload. The order of the checks doesn't matter,
+	// all of them will be started at the same time.
+	AdmissionChecks []string `json:"admissionChecks"`
+}
+
+// WorkloadStatus defines the observed state of Workload
+type WorkloadStatus struct {
+[...]
+	// Status of admission checks, if there are any specified 
+	// for the ClusterQueue in which the workload is queued.
+	AdmissionChecksConditions []metav1.Condition `json:"admissionChecksConditions,omitempty"`
+}
+
+
+// Cluster-scoped top-level object defining a check that 
+// can be referenced in ClusterQueue
+type AdmissionCheck struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta   `json:",inline"`
+	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
+	Spec AdmissionCheckSpec `json:"spec,omitempty"`
+}
+
+const (
+	// The ckech cannot pass at this moment, back off (possibly 
+	// allowing other to try, unblock quota) and retry.
+	Retry metav1.ConditionStatus = "Retry"
+	// The check will not pass in the near future. It is not worth
+	// to retry.
+	Reject metav1.ConditionStatus = "Reject"
+	// The check might pass if there was fewer workloads. Proceed
+	// with any pending workload preemption.
+	QuotaExhausted metav1.ConditionStatus = "QuotaExhausted"
+)
+
+// AdmissionCheckSpec defines the desired state of AdmissionCheck.
+type AdmissionCheckSpec struct {
+	// Name of the controller which will actually perform
+	// the checks. This is the name with which controller indentifies with,
+	// not a K8S pod or deployment name. Cannot be empty. 
+	ControllerName string `json:"controllerName"`
+
+	// How long to keep the workload suspended 
+	// after a failed check (after it transitioned to False).
+	// After that the check state goes to "Unknown".
+	// The default is 15 min. 
+	RetryDelayMinutes *int64. `json:"retryDelayMinutes,omitempty"`
+
+	// A reference to the additional parameters for the check. 
+	Parameters *AdmissionCheckParametersReference `json:"parameters,omitempty"`
+
+	// How should the workload book quota (and possibly preempt others) 
+	// before the check pass. The default is NoBooking.
+	// If different modes are used for different AdmissionChecks,
+	// the most restrictive one is used.
+	QuotaBooking *QuotaBookingMode `json:"quotaBooking,omitempty"`
+}
+
+const (
+	// No booking, unless a check explicitely asks for it reporting quota exhaused.
+	NoBooking QuotaBookingMode = "NoBooking"
+	
+	// Book quota (and preempt) immediately after the basic quota checks 
+	// are done, without waiting for the additional checks to cpmplete.
+	BookAfterQuotaCheck QuotaBookingMode = "BookAfterQuotaCheck"
+)
+
+// Points to where the parameters for the checks are. 
+// As clusterqueue are in cluster scope - this should be
+// a dedicated CRD specific for the Controller.
+type AdmissionCheckParametersReference struct {
+	// ApiGroup is the group for the resource being referenced. 
+	APIGroup string `json:"apiGroup"`
+
+	// Kind is the type of the resource being referenced.
+	Kind string `json:"kind"`
+
+	// Name is the name of the resource being referenced.
+	Name string `json:"name"`
+}
+```
+
+For every workload that is put to a ClusterQueue that has AdmissionChecks
+configured Kueue will add:
+
+* “AdmissionPrecheck” set false to Conditions.
```

  +1 on Marcin. The quota might be violated if we defer preemption.

+# KEP-993: Two Stage Admission Process
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)

+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+This KEP defines the extension point to plug in arbitrary, additional checks
+for workloads before they are admitted for execution. These external checks may
+be implemented inside or outside of Kueue and may provide functionality like
+budgeting, capacity provisioning or some elements of multicluster dispatching.
+
+## Motivation
+
+With the growth of Kueue, not all desired elements may land inside of the core
+Kueue. Some users may even not want to publish their custom admission logic in
+a public repository. At the same time, we don’t want to force users to
+fork Kueue. Thus, an pluggable mechanism for workload admission needs to
+be established.
+
+### Goals
+
+Define mechanism to allow external controllers:
+
+* to give green light to admit a workload.
+* to temporarily hold workload admission.
+* to stop a previously admitted workload and move it back to the
+suspended state.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Provide a specific design or implementation for any external controller.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Extend ClusterQueue definition with a list of external controller names that
+need to give green light to admit a workload. Until all of the controllers, which
+identify with these names, don’t give a green light, the workload will not
+be admitted. 
+
+Each workload that goes to such a queue, will get additional conditions, 
+in a dedicated field in the status, each reflecting the go/no-go 
+decision of each of the external controllers. Once
+a controller is confident that the workload can be admitted, it flips the
+status of the corresponding condition from "Unknown" to "True". 
+
+If a controller changes its mind about a workload, it can switch the condition
+back to false and the workload will be immediately suspended.
+
+### User Stories (Optional)
+
+#### Story 1
+
+I want to use the [Cluster Autoscaler ProvisioningRequest API](https://github.com/kubernetes/autoscaler/pull/5848) 
+to ensure that the resources can be provided in full before starting the workload.  
+
+#### Story 2
+
+I want to base workload admission on budget. I have the actual consumption metrics
+in my Prometheus/Datadog/Stackdriver/whatever monitoring system. And weekly
+budget in a CRD, per namespace. I’m happy to modify some small existing sample
+controller, but I don’t want to fork the whole Kueue to adjust some minor details.
+ 
+### Notes/Constraints/Caveats (Optional)
+
+Each of the go/no-go decisions is best-effort and can be reversed at any time. 
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+## Design Details
+
+TL;DR; 
+* extend ClusterQueueSpec with the list of checks.
+* add extra conditions to Workload status.
+* introduce new CRD, AdmissionCheck.
+
+Details:
+
+We will extend ClusterQueueSpec definition by adding a reference to
+AdmissionChecks that the queue needs to perform before admitting a
+workload. The design of AdmissionChecks is similar to IngressClass
+- it allows passing additional parameters, specific to particular checks
+that need to be performed. 
+
+```
+// ClusterQueueSpec defines the desired state of ClusterQueue.
+type ClusterQueueSpec struct {
+[...]
+	// List of AdmissionCheck names that needs to be passed
+	// to admit a workload. The order of the checks doesn't matter,
+	// all of them will be started at the same time.
+	AdmissionChecks []string `json:"admissionChecks"`
+}
+
+// WorkloadStatus defines the observed state of Workload.
+type WorkloadStatus struct {
+[...]
+	// Status of admission checks, if there are any specified 
+	// for the ClusterQueue in which the workload is queued.
+	AdmissionChecksConditions []metav1.Condition `json:"admissionChecksConditions,omitempty"`
+}
+
+// Condition names used in WorkloadStatus
+const (
+	AdmissionPrecheck string = "AdmissionPrecheck"
+)
+
+// Cluster-scoped top-level object defining a check that 
+// can be referenced in ClusterQueue.
+type AdmissionCheck struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta   `json:",inline"`
+	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
+	Spec AdmissionCheckSpec `json:"spec,omitempty"`
+}
+
+// Condition Reasons used by AdmissionChecks.
+const (
+	// The check cannot pass at this moment, back off (possibly 
+	// allowing other to try, unblock quota) and retry. Can be set only
+	// when Condition status is set to "False"
+	Retry string = "Retry"
+	// The check will not pass in the near future. It is not worth
+	// to retry. Can be set together with Condition status "False".
+	Reject string = "Reject"
+	// The check might pass if there was fewer workloads. Proceed
+	// with any pending workload preemption. Should be set 
+	// when condition status is still "Unknown" 
+	BookQuotaRequired status = "BookQuotaRequired"
+)
+
+// AdmissionCheckSpec defines the desired state of AdmissionCheck.
+type AdmissionCheckSpec struct {
+	// Name of the controller which will actually perform
+	// the checks. This is the name with which controller indentifies with,
+	// not a K8S pod or deployment name. Cannot be empty. 
+	ControllerName string `json:"controllerName"`
+
+	// How long to keep the workload suspended 
+	// after a failed check (after it transitioned to False).
+	// After that the check state goes to "Unknown".
+	// The default is 15 min. 
+	RetryDelayMinutes *int64 `json:"retryDelayMinutes,omitempty"`
+
+	// A reference to the additional parameters for the check. 
+	Parameters *AdmissionCheckParametersReference `json:"parameters,omitempty"`
+
+	// How should the workload book quota (and possibly preempt others) 
+	// before the check pass. The default is NoBooking.
+	// If different modes are used for different AdmissionChecks,
+	// the most restrictive one is used.
+	QuotaBooking *QuotaBookingMode `json:"quotaBooking,omitempty"`
+}
+
+const (
+	// No booking, unless a check explicitely asks for it reporting quota exhausted.
+	NoBooking QuotaBookingMode = "NoBooking"
+	
+	// Book quota (and preempt) immediately after the basic quota checks 
+	// are done, without waiting for the additional checks to cpmplete.
+	BookAfterQuotaCheck QuotaBookingMode = "BookAfterQuotaCheck"
+)
+
+// Points to where the parameters for the checks are. 
+// As clusterqueue are in cluster scope - this should be
+// a dedicated CRD specific for the Controller.
+type AdmissionCheckParametersReference struct {
+	// ApiGroup is the group for the resource being referenced. 
+	APIGroup string `json:"apiGroup"`
+
+	// Kind is the type of the resource being referenced.
+	Kind string `json:"kind"`
+
+	// Name is the name of the resource being referenced.
+	Name string `json:"name"`
+}
+```
+
+For every workload that is put to a ClusterQueue that has AdmissionChecks
+configured Kueue will add:
+
+* “AdmissionPrecheck” set false to Conditions.
+* “<checkName>” set to "Unknown" for each of the AdmissionChecks to AdmissionCheckConditions.
+
+Kueue will perform the very same checks that it does today, 
+before admitting a workload. However, once the basic checks 
+pass AND there are some AdmissionChecks configured, AND the
+workload is not in on-hold retry state from some check, it will:
+
+1. Fill the Admission field in workload, with the desired flavor assignment. 
```

  This should happen before, along with setting AdmissionPrecheck, otherwise we could lose the assignment on a controller restart.
  
  However, at this point, we should set the Admitted condition to true.

+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+## Design Details

+TL;DR; 
+* extend ClusterQueueSpec with the list of checks.
+* add extra conditions to Workload status.
+* introduce new CRD, AdmissionCheck.
+
+Details:

+We will extend ClusterQueueSpec definition by adding a reference to
+AdmissionChecks that the queue needs to perform before admitting a
+workload. The design of AdmissionChecks is similar to IngressClass
+- it allows passing additional parameters, specific to particular checks
+that need to be performed. 
+
+```

+type ClusterQueueSpec struct {
+[...]

+	// to admit a workload. The order of the checks doesn't matter,
+	// all of them will be started at the same time.

+	// for the ClusterQueue in which the workload is queued.
+	AdmissionChecksConditions []metav1.Condition `json:"admissionChecksConditions,omitempty"`

+// can be referenced in ClusterQueue
+type AdmissionCheck struct {

+	// allowing other to try, unblock quota) and retry.

+	// to retry.
+	Reject metav1.ConditionStatus = "Reject"
+	// The check might pass if there was fewer workloads. Proceed
+	// with any pending workload preemption.
+	QuotaExhausted metav1.ConditionStatus = "QuotaExhausted"
+)
+
+// AdmissionCheckSpec defines the desired state of AdmissionCheck.
+type AdmissionCheckSpec struct {
+	// Name of the controller which will actually perform
+	// the checks. This is the name with which controller indentifies with,
+	// not a K8S pod or deployment name. Cannot be empty. 
+	ControllerName string `json:"controllerName"`
+
+	// How long to keep the workload suspended 
+	// after a failed check (after it transitioned to False).
+	// After that the check state goes to "Unknown".
+	// The default is 15 min. 
+	RetryDelayMinutes *int64. `json:"retryDelayMinutes,omitempty"`
+
+	// A reference to the additional parameters for the check. 
+	Parameters *AdmissionCheckParametersReference `json:"parameters,omitempty"`
+
+	// How should the workload book quota (and possibly preempt others) 
+	// before the check pass. The default is NoBooking.
+	// If different modes are used for different AdmissionChecks,
+	// the most restrictive one is used.
+	QuotaBooking *QuotaBookingMode `json:"quotaBooking,omitempty"`
+}
+
+const (
+	// No booking, unless a check explicitely asks for it reporting quota exhaused.
+	NoBooking QuotaBookingMode = "NoBooking"
+	
+	// Book quota (and preempt) immediately after the basic quota checks 
+	// are done, without waiting for the additional checks to cpmplete.
+	BookAfterQuotaCheck QuotaBookingMode = "BookAfterQuotaCheck"
+)
+
+// Points to where the parameters for the checks are. 
+// As clusterqueue are in cluster scope - this should be
+// a dedicated CRD specific for the Controller.
+type AdmissionCheckParametersReference struct {
+	// ApiGroup is the group for the resource being referenced. 
+	APIGroup string `json:"apiGroup"`
+
+	// Kind is the type of the resource being referenced.
+	Kind string `json:"kind"`
+
+	// Name is the name of the resource being referenced.
+	Name string `json:"name"`
+}
+```
+
+For every workload that is put to a ClusterQueue that has AdmissionChecks
+configured Kueue will add:
+
+* “AdmissionPrecheck” set false to Conditions.
```

  Actually, to follow https://github.com/kubernetes/community/blob/master/contributors/devel/sig-architecture/api-conventions.md#typical-status-properties,
  It should be AdmissionPrechecked

### Review by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) (commented) — 2023-08-23T17:12:28Z

- **keps/993-two-phase-admission/README.md:210** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-08-23T17:12:27Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,280 @@
+# KEP-993: Two Stage Admission Process
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories (Optional)](#user-stories-optional)
+    - [Story 1](#story-1)
+    - [Story 2](#story-2)
+  - [Notes/Constraints/Caveats (Optional)](#notesconstraintscaveats-optional)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+      - [Prerequisite testing updates](#prerequisite-testing-updates)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+This KEP defines the extension point to plug in arbitrary, additional checks
+for workloads before they are admitted for execution. These external checks may
+be implemented inside or outside of Kueue and may provide functionality like
+budgeting, capacity provisioning or some elements of multicluster dispatching.
+
+## Motivation
+
+With the growth of Kueue, not all desired elements may land inside of the core
+Kueue. Some users may even not want to publish their custom admission logic in
+a public repository. At the same time, we don’t want to force users to
+fork Kueue. Thus, an pluggable mechanism for workload admission needs to
+be established.
+
+### Goals
+
+Define mechanism to allow external controllers:
+
+* to give green light to admit a workload.
+* to temporarily hold workload admission.
+* to stop a previously admitted workload and move it back to the
+suspended state.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Provide a specific design or implementation for any external controller.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Extend ClusterQueue definition with a list of external controller names that
+need to give green light to admit a workload. Until all of the controllers, which
+identify with these names, don’t give a green light, the workload will not
+be admitted. 
+
+Each workload that goes to such a queue, will get additional conditions, 
+in a dedicated field in the status, each reflecting the go/no-go 
+decision of each of the external controllers. Once
+a controller is confident that the workload can be admitted, it flips the
+status of the corresponding condition from "Unknown" to "True". 
+
+If a controller changes its mind about a workload, it can switch the condition
+back to false and the workload will be immediately suspended.
+
+### User Stories (Optional)
+
+#### Story 1
+
+I want to use the [Cluster Autoscaler ProvisioningRequest API](https://github.com/kubernetes/autoscaler/pull/5848) 
+to ensure that the resources can be provided in full before starting the workload.  
+
+#### Story 2
+
+I want to base workload admission on budget. I have the actual consumption metrics
+in my Prometheus/Datadog/Stackdriver/whatever monitoring system. And weekly
+budget in a CRD, per namespace. I’m happy to modify some small existing sample
+controller, but I don’t want to fork the whole Kueue to adjust some minor details.
+ 
+### Notes/Constraints/Caveats (Optional)
+
+Each of the go/no-go decisions is best-effort and can be reversed at any time. 
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+## Design Details
+
+TL;DR; 
+* extend ClusterQueueSpec with the list of checks.
+* add extra conditions to Workload status.
+* introduce new CRD, AdmissionCheck.
+
+Details:
+
+We will extend ClusterQueueSpec definition by adding a reference to
+AdmissionChecks that the queue needs to perform before admitting a
+workload. The design of AdmissionChecks is similar to IngressClass
+- it allows passing additional parameters, specific to particular checks
+that need to be performed. 
+
+```
+// ClusterQueueSpec defines the desired state of ClusterQueue.
+type ClusterQueueSpec struct {
+[...]
+	// List of AdmissionCheck names that needs to be passed
+	// to admit a workload. The order of the checks doesn't matter,
+	// all of them will be started at the same time.
+	AdmissionChecks []string `json:"admissionChecks"`
+}
+
+// WorkloadStatus defines the observed state of Workload.
+type WorkloadStatus struct {
+[...]
+	// Status of admission checks, if there are any specified 
+	// for the ClusterQueue in which the workload is queued.
+	AdmissionChecksConditions []metav1.Condition `json:"admissionChecksConditions,omitempty"`
+}
+
+// Condition names used in WorkloadStatus
+const (
+	AdmissionPrecheck string = "AdmissionPrecheck"
+)
+
+// Cluster-scoped top-level object defining a check that 
+// can be referenced in ClusterQueue.
+type AdmissionCheck struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta   `json:",inline"`
+	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
+	Spec AdmissionCheckSpec `json:"spec,omitempty"`
+}
+
+// Condition Reasons used by AdmissionChecks.
+const (
+	// The check cannot pass at this moment, back off (possibly 
+	// allowing other to try, unblock quota) and retry. Can be set only
+	// when Condition status is set to "False"
+	Retry string = "Retry"
+	// The check will not pass in the near future. It is not worth
+	// to retry. Can be set together with Condition status "False".
+	Reject string = "Reject"
+	// The check might pass if there was fewer workloads. Proceed
+	// with any pending workload preemption. Should be set 
+	// when condition status is still "Unknown" 
+	BookQuotaRequired status = "BookQuotaRequired"
+)
+
+// AdmissionCheckSpec defines the desired state of AdmissionCheck.
+type AdmissionCheckSpec struct {
+	// Name of the controller which will actually perform
+	// the checks. This is the name with which controller indentifies with,
+	// not a K8S pod or deployment name. Cannot be empty. 
+	ControllerName string `json:"controllerName"`
+
+	// How long to keep the workload suspended 
+	// after a failed check (after it transitioned to False).
+	// After that the check state goes to "Unknown".
+	// The default is 15 min. 
+	RetryDelayMinutes *int64 `json:"retryDelayMinutes,omitempty"`
+
+	// A reference to the additional parameters for the check. 
+	Parameters *AdmissionCheckParametersReference `json:"parameters,omitempty"`
+
+	// How should the workload book quota (and possibly preempt others) 
+	// before the check pass. The default is NoBooking.
+	// If different modes are used for different AdmissionChecks,
+	// the most restrictive one is used.
+	QuotaBooking *QuotaBookingMode `json:"quotaBooking,omitempty"`
+}
+
+const (
+	// No booking, unless a check explicitely asks for it reporting quota exhausted.
+	NoBooking QuotaBookingMode = "NoBooking"
+	
+	// Book quota (and preempt) immediately after the basic quota checks 
+	// are done, without waiting for the additional checks to cpmplete.
+	BookAfterQuotaCheck QuotaBookingMode = "BookAfterQuotaCheck"
+)
+
+// Points to where the parameters for the checks are. 
+// As clusterqueue are in cluster scope - this should be
+// a dedicated CRD specific for the Controller.
+type AdmissionCheckParametersReference struct {
+	// ApiGroup is the group for the resource being referenced. 
+	APIGroup string `json:"apiGroup"`
+
+	// Kind is the type of the resource being referenced.
+	Kind string `json:"kind"`
+
+	// Name is the name of the resource being referenced.
+	Name string `json:"name"`
+}
+```
+
+For every workload that is put to a ClusterQueue that has AdmissionChecks
+configured Kueue will add:
+
+* “AdmissionPrecheck” set false to Conditions.
+* “<checkName>” set to "Unknown" for each of the AdmissionChecks to AdmissionCheckConditions.
+
+Kueue will perform the very same checks that it does today, 
+before admitting a workload. However, once the basic checks 
+pass AND there are some AdmissionChecks configured, AND the
+workload is not in on-hold retry state from some check, it will:
+
+1. Fill the Admission field in workload, with the desired flavor assignment. 
```

  Nvm, I got confused with the paragraphs.
  
  The current proposal makes sense.

  From @trasc in https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/1075#discussion_r1303223834
  
  > There are two reasons why I don't think it's a good idea:
  
  > 1. This can imply that is done before the checks.
  
  This is true. We want a Condition that, when true, `admissionChecks` can start.
  
  > 2. I think, the Precheck, as described in the KEP is not blocking the quota
  
  Correct, and that's why naming it QuotaReserved doesn't seem accurate. Unless you are suggesting having 3 conditions?
  Can you elaborate?

+# KEP-993: Two Stage Admission Process
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)

+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)

+* “AdmissionPrecheck” set false to Conditions.
```

  > This is true. We want a Condition that, when true, `admissionChecks` can start.
  
  There is no reason to block the admissionCheck until the Quota is reserved/checked, a controller can choose to do it only after, but i don't see any value forcing this.
  
  > Correct, and that's why naming it QuotaReserved doesn't seem accurate. Unless you are suggesting having 3 conditions?
  Can you elaborate?
  
  In #1045 having the condition (which is still called Admitted there, #1075 only renames it) means that the quota is blocked for the workload in question. 
  
   Now, if there is a usecase in which a check controller needs to know that at some point in the past the workload wold have had the option to block the quota, what it could do is. 
  
  1. Keep it's condition in a non False state (preferably Unknown)
  2. The scheduler will reserve the quota at some point. 
  3. The controller can switch it's condition to false. (this will cancel the quota reservation)
  4. Perform it's check. And set its condition to True.
  5. The workload will go into the scheduling again.
  
  (if the controller has a quick way of doing the check in some cases, the reservation cancelling and the second scheduling can be skipped)

### Review by [@mwielgus](https://github.com/mwielgus) (commented) — 2023-08-24T08:38:28Z

- **keps/993-two-phase-admission/README.md:181** by [@mwielgus](https://github.com/mwielgus) — 2023-08-24T08:38:28Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,280 @@
+# KEP-993: Two Stage Admission Process
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories (Optional)](#user-stories-optional)
+    - [Story 1](#story-1)
+    - [Story 2](#story-2)
+  - [Notes/Constraints/Caveats (Optional)](#notesconstraintscaveats-optional)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+      - [Prerequisite testing updates](#prerequisite-testing-updates)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+This KEP defines the extension point to plug in arbitrary, additional checks
+for workloads before they are admitted for execution. These external checks may
+be implemented inside or outside of Kueue and may provide functionality like
+budgeting, capacity provisioning or some elements of multicluster dispatching.
+
+## Motivation
+
+With the growth of Kueue, not all desired elements may land inside of the core
+Kueue. Some users may even not want to publish their custom admission logic in
+a public repository. At the same time, we don’t want to force users to
+fork Kueue. Thus, an pluggable mechanism for workload admission needs to
+be established.
+
+### Goals
+
+Define mechanism to allow external controllers:
+
+* to give green light to admit a workload.
+* to temporarily hold workload admission.
+* to stop a previously admitted workload and move it back to the
+suspended state.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Provide a specific design or implementation for any external controller.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Extend ClusterQueue definition with a list of external controller names that
+need to give green light to admit a workload. Until all of the controllers, which
+identify with these names, don’t give a green light, the workload will not
+be admitted. 
+
+Each workload that goes to such a queue, will get additional conditions, 
+in a dedicated field in the status, each reflecting the go/no-go 
+decision of each of the external controllers. Once
+a controller is confident that the workload can be admitted, it flips the
+status of the corresponding condition from "Unknown" to "True". 
+
+If a controller changes its mind about a workload, it can switch the condition
+back to false and the workload will be immediately suspended.
+
+### User Stories (Optional)
+
+#### Story 1
+
+I want to use the [Cluster Autoscaler ProvisioningRequest API](https://github.com/kubernetes/autoscaler/pull/5848) 
+to ensure that the resources can be provided in full before starting the workload.  
+
+#### Story 2
+
+I want to base workload admission on budget. I have the actual consumption metrics
+in my Prometheus/Datadog/Stackdriver/whatever monitoring system. And weekly
+budget in a CRD, per namespace. I’m happy to modify some small existing sample
+controller, but I don’t want to fork the whole Kueue to adjust some minor details.
+ 
+### Notes/Constraints/Caveats (Optional)
+
+Each of the go/no-go decisions is best-effort and can be reversed at any time. 
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+## Design Details
+
+TL;DR; 
+* extend ClusterQueueSpec with the list of checks.
+* add extra conditions to Workload status.
+* introduce new CRD, AdmissionCheck.
+
+Details:
+
+We will extend ClusterQueueSpec definition by adding a reference to
+AdmissionChecks that the queue needs to perform before admitting a
+workload. The design of AdmissionChecks is similar to IngressClass
+- it allows passing additional parameters, specific to particular checks
+that need to be performed. 
+
+```
+// ClusterQueueSpec defines the desired state of ClusterQueue.
+type ClusterQueueSpec struct {
+[...]
+	// List of AdmissionCheck names that needs to be passed
+	// to admit a workload. The order of the checks doesn't matter,
+	// all of them will be started at the same time.
+	AdmissionChecks []string `json:"admissionChecks"`
+}
+
+// WorkloadStatus defines the observed state of Workload.
+type WorkloadStatus struct {
+[...]
+	// Status of admission checks, if there are any specified 
+	// for the ClusterQueue in which the workload is queued.
+	AdmissionChecksConditions []metav1.Condition `json:"admissionChecksConditions,omitempty"`
+}
+
+// Condition names used in WorkloadStatus
+const (
+	AdmissionPrecheck string = "AdmissionPrecheck"
+)
+
+// Cluster-scoped top-level object defining a check that 
+// can be referenced in ClusterQueue.
+type AdmissionCheck struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta   `json:",inline"`
+	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
+	Spec AdmissionCheckSpec `json:"spec,omitempty"`
+}
+
+// Condition Reasons used by AdmissionChecks.
+const (
+	// The check cannot pass at this moment, back off (possibly 
+	// allowing other to try, unblock quota) and retry. Can be set only
+	// when Condition status is set to "False"
+	Retry string = "Retry"
+	// The check will not pass in the near future. It is not worth
+	// to retry. Can be set together with Condition status "False".
+	Reject string = "Reject"
+	// The check might pass if there was fewer workloads. Proceed
+	// with any pending workload preemption. Should be set 
+	// when condition status is still "Unknown" 
+	BookQuotaRequired status = "BookQuotaRequired"
+)
+
+// AdmissionCheckSpec defines the desired state of AdmissionCheck.
+type AdmissionCheckSpec struct {
+	// Name of the controller which will actually perform
+	// the checks. This is the name with which controller indentifies with,
+	// not a K8S pod or deployment name. Cannot be empty. 
+	ControllerName string `json:"controllerName"`
+
+	// How long to keep the workload suspended 
+	// after a failed check (after it transitioned to False).
+	// After that the check state goes to "Unknown".
+	// The default is 15 min. 
+	RetryDelayMinutes *int64 `json:"retryDelayMinutes,omitempty"`
+
+	// A reference to the additional parameters for the check. 
+	Parameters *AdmissionCheckParametersReference `json:"parameters,omitempty"`
+
+	// How should the workload book quota (and possibly preempt others) 
+	// before the check pass. The default is NoBooking.
+	// If different modes are used for different AdmissionChecks,
+	// the most restrictive one is used.
+	QuotaBooking *QuotaBookingMode `json:"quotaBooking,omitempty"`
+}
+
+const (
+	// No booking, unless a check explicitely asks for it reporting quota exhausted.
+	NoBooking QuotaBookingMode = "NoBooking"
+	
+	// Book quota (and preempt) immediately after the basic quota checks 
+	// are done, without waiting for the additional checks to cpmplete.
+	BookAfterQuotaCheck QuotaBookingMode = "BookAfterQuotaCheck"
```

  That is potentially misleading. Some "NoBooking" checks may be executed after the booking has actually been done.

### Review by [@mwielgus](https://github.com/mwielgus) (commented) — 2023-08-24T08:47:57Z

### Review by [@mwielgus](https://github.com/mwielgus) (commented) — 2023-08-24T08:48:30Z

- **keps/993-two-phase-admission/README.md:221** by [@mwielgus](https://github.com/mwielgus) — 2023-08-24T08:48:29Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,226 @@
+# KEP-993: Two Stage Admission Process
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories (Optional)](#user-stories-optional)
+    - [Story 1](#story-1)
+    - [Story 2](#story-2)
+  - [Notes/Constraints/Caveats (Optional)](#notesconstraintscaveats-optional)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+      - [Prerequisite testing updates](#prerequisite-testing-updates)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+This KEP defines the extension point to plug in arbitrary, additional checks
+for workloads before they are admitted for execution. These external checks may
+be implemented inside or outside of Kueue and may provide functionality like
+budgeting, capacity provisioning or some elements of multicluster dispatching.
+
+## Motivation
+
+With the growth of Kueue, not all desired elements may land inside of the core
+Kueue. Some users may even not want to publish their custom admission logic in
+a public repository. At the same time, we don’t want to force users to
+fork Kueue. Thus, an pluggable mechanism for workload admission needs to
+be established.
+
+### Goals
+
+Define mechanism to allow external controllers:
+
+* to give green light to admit a workload.
+* to temporarily hold workload admission.
+* to stop a previously admitted workload and move it back to the
+suspended state.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Provide a specific design or implementation for any external controller.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Extend ClusterQueue definition with a list of external controller names that
+need to give green light to admit a workload. Until all of the controllers, which
+identify with these names, don’t give a green light, the workload will not
+be admitted. 
+
+Each workload that goes to such a queue, will get additional conditions, each
+reflecting the go/no-go decision of each of the external controllers. Once
+a controller is confident that the workload can be admitted, it flips the
+status of the corresponding condition from false to true. 
+
+If a controller changes its mind about a workload, it can switch the condition
+back to false and the workload will be immediately suspended.
+
+### User Stories (Optional)
+
+#### Story 1
+
+I want to use the [Cluster Autoscaler ProvisioningRequest API](https://github.com/kubernetes/autoscaler/pull/5848) 
+to ensure that the resources can be provided in full before starting the workload.  
+
+#### Story 2
+
+I want to base workload admission on budget. I have the actual consumption metrics
+in my Prometheus/Datadog/Stackdriver/whatever monitoring system. And weekly
+budget in a CRD, per namespace. I’m happy to modify some small existing sample
+controller, but I don’t want to fork the whole Kueue to adjust some minor details.
+ 
+### Notes/Constraints/Caveats (Optional)
+
+Each of the go/no-go decisions is best-effort and can be reversed at any time. 
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+## Design Details
+
+We will extend ClusterQueueSpec definition by adding a reference to
+AdmissionChecks that the queue needs to perform before admitting a
+workload. The design of AdmissionChecks is similar to IngressClass
+- it allows passing additional parameters, specific to particular checks
+that need to be performed. 
+
+```
+// ClusterQueueSpec defines the desired state of ClusterQueue
+type ClusterQueueSpec struct {
+[...]
+	// List of AdmissionCheck names that needs to be passed
+	// to admit a workload.  
+	AdmissionChecks []string `json:"addotomalChecks"`
+}
+
+
+// Cluster-scoped top-level object defining a check that 
+// can be referenced in ClusterQueue
+type AdmissionCheck struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta   `json:",inline"`
+	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
+	Spec AdmissionCheckSpec `json:"spec,omitempty"`
+}
+
+const (
+	Retry CheckFailureState = “Retry”
+	Reject CheckFailureState = “Reject”
+)
+
+type AdmissionCheckSpec struct {
+// Name of the controller which will actually perform
+// the checks. Cannot be empty.
+	ControllerName string `json:"controllerName"`
+
+	// How long to keep the workload suspended 
+	// after a failed check.
+	RetryDelayMinutes *int64. `json:"retryDelayMinutes,omitempty"`
+
+	// A reference to the additional parameters for the check. 
+	Parameters *AdmissionCheckParametersReference `json:"parameters,omitempty"`
+}
+
+// Points to where the parameters for the checks are. 
+// As clusterqueue are in cluster scope - this should be
+// a dedicated CRD specific for the Controller.
+type AdmissionCheckParametersReference struct {
+	// ApiGroup is the group for the resource being referenced. 
+	APIGroup string `json:"apiGroup"`
+
+	// Kind is the type of the resource being referenced.
+	Kind string `json:"kind""`
+
+	// Name is the name of the resource being referenced.
+	Name string `json:"name"`
+}
+```
+
+For every workload that is put to a ClusterQueue, Kueue will perform the very 
+same checks that it does today, before admitting a workload. However, once the basic checks pass AND there are some AdmissionChecks configured, AND the workload is not in on-hold retry state from some check, it will:
+
+1. Fill the Admission field in workload, with the desired flavor assignment. 
+2. Not do any preemptions yet.
+3. Set conditions on the workload:
+* “AdmissionPrecheck” to true
+* “AdmissionCheck|<checkName>” to unknown for each of the add
+
+Kueue will only pass as many pods past AdmissionPrecheck as there would
+fit in the quota together, possibly limited by a Kueue configuration option.
+That would violate a bit BestEffort logic of queues - if there is 1000 tasks
+in a queue that doesn’t pass quota and 1001st task passes, the best effort
+queue would let it in. BestEffort queue with 1000 tasks that don’t pass
+AdditioanlChecks would not let 1001st task in (it will not reach the
+checks). Without this limitation, a large number of tasks could be switched
+back and forth from Precheck to suspended state. 
```

  Ack.

### Review by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) (commented) — 2023-08-24T14:20:12Z

- **keps/993-two-phase-admission/README.md:202** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-08-24T14:20:12Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,274 @@

+type AdmissionCheck struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta   `json:",inline"`
+	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
+	Spec AdmissionCheckSpec `json:"spec,omitempty"`
+}
+
+const (
+	// The ckech cannot pass at this moment, back off (possibly 
+	// allowing other to try, unblock quota) and retry.
+	Retry metav1.ConditionStatus = "Retry"
+	// The check will not pass in the near future. It is not worth
+	// to retry.
+	Reject metav1.ConditionStatus = "Reject"
+	// The check might pass if there was fewer workloads. Proceed
+	// with any pending workload preemption.
+	QuotaExhausted metav1.ConditionStatus = "QuotaExhausted"
+)
+
+// AdmissionCheckSpec defines the desired state of AdmissionCheck.
+type AdmissionCheckSpec struct {
+	// Name of the controller which will actually perform
+	// the checks. This is the name with which controller indentifies with,
+	// not a K8S pod or deployment name. Cannot be empty. 
+	ControllerName string `json:"controllerName"`
+
+	// How long to keep the workload suspended 
+	// after a failed check (after it transitioned to False).
+	// After that the check state goes to "Unknown".
+	// The default is 15 min. 
+	RetryDelayMinutes *int64. `json:"retryDelayMinutes,omitempty"`
+
+	// A reference to the additional parameters for the check. 
+	Parameters *AdmissionCheckParametersReference `json:"parameters,omitempty"`
+
+	// How should the workload book quota (and possibly preempt others) 
+	// before the check pass. The default is NoBooking.
+	// If different modes are used for different AdmissionChecks,
+	// the most restrictive one is used.
+	QuotaBooking *QuotaBookingMode `json:"quotaBooking,omitempty"`
+}
+
+const (
+	// No booking, unless a check explicitely asks for it reporting quota exhaused.
+	NoBooking QuotaBookingMode = "NoBooking"
+	
+	// Book quota (and preempt) immediately after the basic quota checks 
+	// are done, without waiting for the additional checks to cpmplete.
+	BookAfterQuotaCheck QuotaBookingMode = "BookAfterQuotaCheck"
+)
+
+// Points to where the parameters for the checks are. 
+// As clusterqueue are in cluster scope - this should be
+// a dedicated CRD specific for the Controller.
+type AdmissionCheckParametersReference struct {
+	// ApiGroup is the group for the resource being referenced. 
+	APIGroup string `json:"apiGroup"`
+
+	// Kind is the type of the resource being referenced.
+	Kind string `json:"kind"`
+
+	// Name is the name of the resource being referenced.
+	Name string `json:"name"`
+}
+```
+
+For every workload that is put to a ClusterQueue that has AdmissionChecks
+configured Kueue will add:
+
+* “AdmissionPrecheck” set false to Conditions.
```

  Let's recap.
  In implementation terms, what we need is a condition that indicates that Kueue has executed the scheduling cycle and, if necessary, found candidates for preemption.
  
  Preemption might or might not happen at this point, depending on what is set in `quotaBooking` . If this setting says `NoBooking`, meaning that we shouldn't do preemption, then it doesn't make sense to call the condition `QuotaReserved`.
  
  `PreCheck` is a bit more neutral, although a bit vague. Let me think about it more.

### Review by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) (commented) — 2023-08-24T15:28:54Z

- **keps/993-two-phase-admission/README.md:202** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2023-08-24T15:28:54Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,274 @@
+# KEP-993: Two Stage Admission Process
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories (Optional)](#user-stories-optional)
+    - [Story 1](#story-1)
+    - [Story 2](#story-2)
+  - [Notes/Constraints/Caveats (Optional)](#notesconstraintscaveats-optional)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+      - [Prerequisite testing updates](#prerequisite-testing-updates)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+This KEP defines the extension point to plug in arbitrary, additional checks
+for workloads before they are admitted for execution. These external checks may
+be implemented inside or outside of Kueue and may provide functionality like
+budgeting, capacity provisioning or some elements of multicluster dispatching.
+
+## Motivation
+
+With the growth of Kueue, not all desired elements may land inside of the core
+Kueue. Some users may even not want to publish their custom admission logic in
+a public repository. At the same time, we don’t want to force users to
+fork Kueue. Thus, an pluggable mechanism for workload admission needs to
+be established.
+
+### Goals
+
+Define mechanism to allow external controllers:
+
+* to give green light to admit a workload.
+* to temporarily hold workload admission.
+* to stop a previously admitted workload and move it back to the
+suspended state.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Provide a specific design or implementation for any external controller.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Extend ClusterQueue definition with a list of external controller names that
+need to give green light to admit a workload. Until all of the controllers, which
+identify with these names, don’t give a green light, the workload will not
+be admitted. 
+
+Each workload that goes to such a queue, will get additional conditions, 
+in a dedicated field in the status, each reflecting the go/no-go 
+decision of each of the external controllers. Once
+a controller is confident that the workload can be admitted, it flips the
+status of the corresponding condition from false to true. 
+
+If a controller changes its mind about a workload, it can switch the condition
+back to false and the workload will be immediately suspended.
+
+### User Stories (Optional)
+
+#### Story 1
+
+I want to use the [Cluster Autoscaler ProvisioningRequest API](https://github.com/kubernetes/autoscaler/pull/5848) 
+to ensure that the resources can be provided in full before starting the workload.  
+
+#### Story 2
+
+I want to base workload admission on budget. I have the actual consumption metrics
+in my Prometheus/Datadog/Stackdriver/whatever monitoring system. And weekly
+budget in a CRD, per namespace. I’m happy to modify some small existing sample
+controller, but I don’t want to fork the whole Kueue to adjust some minor details.
+ 
+### Notes/Constraints/Caveats (Optional)
+
+Each of the go/no-go decisions is best-effort and can be reversed at any time. 
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+## Design Details
+
+TL;DR; 
+* extend ClusterQueueSpec with the list of checks.
+* add extra conditions to Workload status.
+* introduce new CRD, AdmissionCheck.
+
+Details:
+
+We will extend ClusterQueueSpec definition by adding a reference to
+AdmissionChecks that the queue needs to perform before admitting a
+workload. The design of AdmissionChecks is similar to IngressClass
+- it allows passing additional parameters, specific to particular checks
+that need to be performed. 
+
+```
+// ClusterQueueSpec defines the desired state of ClusterQueue
+type ClusterQueueSpec struct {
+[...]
+	// List of AdmissionCheck names that needs to be passed
+	// to admit a workload. The order of the checks doesn't matter,
+	// all of them will be started at the same time.
+	AdmissionChecks []string `json:"admissionChecks"`
+}
+
+// WorkloadStatus defines the observed state of Workload
+type WorkloadStatus struct {
+[...]
+	// Status of admission checks, if there are any specified 
+	// for the ClusterQueue in which the workload is queued.
+	AdmissionChecksConditions []metav1.Condition `json:"admissionChecksConditions,omitempty"`
+}
+
+
+// Cluster-scoped top-level object defining a check that 
+// can be referenced in ClusterQueue
+type AdmissionCheck struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta   `json:",inline"`
+	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
+	Spec AdmissionCheckSpec `json:"spec,omitempty"`
+}
+
+const (
+	// The ckech cannot pass at this moment, back off (possibly 
+	// allowing other to try, unblock quota) and retry.
+	Retry metav1.ConditionStatus = "Retry"
+	// The check will not pass in the near future. It is not worth
+	// to retry.
+	Reject metav1.ConditionStatus = "Reject"
+	// The check might pass if there was fewer workloads. Proceed
+	// with any pending workload preemption.
+	QuotaExhausted metav1.ConditionStatus = "QuotaExhausted"
+)
+
+// AdmissionCheckSpec defines the desired state of AdmissionCheck.
+type AdmissionCheckSpec struct {
+	// Name of the controller which will actually perform
+	// the checks. This is the name with which controller indentifies with,
+	// not a K8S pod or deployment name. Cannot be empty. 
+	ControllerName string `json:"controllerName"`
+
+	// How long to keep the workload suspended 
+	// after a failed check (after it transitioned to False).
+	// After that the check state goes to "Unknown".
+	// The default is 15 min. 
+	RetryDelayMinutes *int64. `json:"retryDelayMinutes,omitempty"`
+
+	// A reference to the additional parameters for the check. 
+	Parameters *AdmissionCheckParametersReference `json:"parameters,omitempty"`
+
+	// How should the workload book quota (and possibly preempt others) 
+	// before the check pass. The default is NoBooking.
+	// If different modes are used for different AdmissionChecks,
+	// the most restrictive one is used.
+	QuotaBooking *QuotaBookingMode `json:"quotaBooking,omitempty"`
+}
+
+const (
+	// No booking, unless a check explicitely asks for it reporting quota exhaused.
+	NoBooking QuotaBookingMode = "NoBooking"
+	
+	// Book quota (and preempt) immediately after the basic quota checks 
+	// are done, without waiting for the additional checks to cpmplete.
+	BookAfterQuotaCheck QuotaBookingMode = "BookAfterQuotaCheck"
+)
+
+// Points to where the parameters for the checks are. 
+// As clusterqueue are in cluster scope - this should be
+// a dedicated CRD specific for the Controller.
+type AdmissionCheckParametersReference struct {
+	// ApiGroup is the group for the resource being referenced. 
+	APIGroup string `json:"apiGroup"`
+
+	// Kind is the type of the resource being referenced.
+	Kind string `json:"kind"`
+
+	// Name is the name of the resource being referenced.
+	Name string `json:"name"`
+}
+```
+
+For every workload that is put to a ClusterQueue that has AdmissionChecks
+configured Kueue will add:
+
+* “AdmissionPrecheck” set false to Conditions.
```

  How about `NominatedForAdmission`?
  - It goes along with the fact that we fill up the `admissionField`.
  - It doesn't give any indication that `admissionChecks` run before or after.
  - It doesn't give any indication about whether preemption happened or quota is reserved.

@@ -0,0 +1,280 @@
+# KEP-993: Two Stage Admission Process
+
+<!-- toc -->
+- [Summary](#summary)
+- [Motivation](#motivation)
+  - [Goals](#goals)
+  - [Non-Goals](#non-goals)
+- [Proposal](#proposal)
+  - [User Stories (Optional)](#user-stories-optional)
+    - [Story 1](#story-1)
+    - [Story 2](#story-2)
+  - [Notes/Constraints/Caveats (Optional)](#notesconstraintscaveats-optional)
+  - [Risks and Mitigations](#risks-and-mitigations)
+- [Design Details](#design-details)
+  - [Test Plan](#test-plan)
+      - [Prerequisite testing updates](#prerequisite-testing-updates)
+    - [Unit Tests](#unit-tests)
+    - [Integration tests](#integration-tests)
+  - [Graduation Criteria](#graduation-criteria)
+- [Implementation History](#implementation-history)
+- [Drawbacks](#drawbacks)
+- [Alternatives](#alternatives)
+<!-- /toc -->
+
+## Summary
+
+This KEP defines the extension point to plug in arbitrary, additional checks
+for workloads before they are admitted for execution. These external checks may
+be implemented inside or outside of Kueue and may provide functionality like
+budgeting, capacity provisioning or some elements of multicluster dispatching.
+
+## Motivation
+
+With the growth of Kueue, not all desired elements may land inside of the core
+Kueue. Some users may even not want to publish their custom admission logic in
+a public repository. At the same time, we don’t want to force users to
+fork Kueue. Thus, an pluggable mechanism for workload admission needs to
+be established.
+
+### Goals
+
+Define mechanism to allow external controllers:
+
+* to give green light to admit a workload.
+* to temporarily hold workload admission.
+* to stop a previously admitted workload and move it back to the
+suspended state.
+
+### Non-Goals
+
+Provide a specific design or implementation for any external controller.
+
+## Proposal
+
+Extend ClusterQueue definition with a list of external controller names that
+need to give green light to admit a workload. Until all of the controllers, which
+identify with these names, don’t give a green light, the workload will not
+be admitted. 
+
+Each workload that goes to such a queue, will get additional conditions, 
+in a dedicated field in the status, each reflecting the go/no-go 
+decision of each of the external controllers. Once
+a controller is confident that the workload can be admitted, it flips the
+status of the corresponding condition from "Unknown" to "True". 
+
+If a controller changes its mind about a workload, it can switch the condition
+back to false and the workload will be immediately suspended.
+
+### User Stories (Optional)
+
+#### Story 1
+
+I want to use the [Cluster Autoscaler ProvisioningRequest API](https://github.com/kubernetes/autoscaler/pull/5848) 
+to ensure that the resources can be provided in full before starting the workload.  
+
+#### Story 2
+
+I want to base workload admission on budget. I have the actual consumption metrics
+in my Prometheus/Datadog/Stackdriver/whatever monitoring system. And weekly
+budget in a CRD, per namespace. I’m happy to modify some small existing sample
+controller, but I don’t want to fork the whole Kueue to adjust some minor details.
+ 
+### Notes/Constraints/Caveats (Optional)
+
+Each of the go/no-go decisions is best-effort and can be reversed at any time. 
+
+### Risks and Mitigations
+
+## Design Details
+
+TL;DR; 
+* extend ClusterQueueSpec with the list of checks.
+* add extra conditions to Workload status.
+* introduce new CRD, AdmissionCheck.
+
+Details:
+
+We will extend ClusterQueueSpec definition by adding a reference to
+AdmissionChecks that the queue needs to perform before admitting a
+workload. The design of AdmissionChecks is similar to IngressClass
+- it allows passing additional parameters, specific to particular checks
+that need to be performed. 
+
+```
+// ClusterQueueSpec defines the desired state of ClusterQueue.
+type ClusterQueueSpec struct {
+[...]
+	// List of AdmissionCheck names that needs to be passed
+	// to admit a workload. The order of the checks doesn't matter,
+	// all of them will be started at the same time.
+	AdmissionChecks []string `json:"admissionChecks"`
+}
+
+// WorkloadStatus defines the observed state of Workload.
+type WorkloadStatus struct {
+[...]
+	// Status of admission checks, if there are any specified 
+	// for the ClusterQueue in which the workload is queued.
+	AdmissionChecksConditions []metav1.Condition `json:"admissionChecksConditions,omitempty"`
+}
+
+// Condition names used in WorkloadStatus
+const (
+	AdmissionPrecheck string = "AdmissionPrecheck"
+)
+
+// Cluster-scoped top-level object defining a check that 
+// can be referenced in ClusterQueue.
+type AdmissionCheck struct {
+	metav1.TypeMeta   `json:",inline"`
+	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
+	Spec AdmissionCheckSpec `json:"spec,omitempty"`
+}
+
+// Condition Reasons used by AdmissionChecks.
+const (
+	// The check cannot pass at this moment, back off (possibly 
+	// allowing other to try, unblock quota) and retry. Can be set only
+	// when Condition status is set to "False"
+	Retry string = "Retry"
+	// The check will not pass in the near future. It is not worth
+	// to retry. Can be set together with Condition status "False".
+	Reject string = "Reject"
+	// The check might pass if there was fewer workloads. Proceed
+	// with any pending workload preemption. Should be set 
+	// when condition status is still "Unknown" 
+	BookQuotaRequired status = "BookQuotaRequired"
+)
+
+// AdmissionCheckSpec defines the desired state of AdmissionCheck.
+type AdmissionCheckSpec struct {
+	// Name of the controller which will actually perform
+	// the checks. This is the name with which controller indentifies with,
+	// not a K8S pod or deployment name. Cannot be empty. 
+	ControllerName string `json:"controllerName"`
+
+	// How long to keep the workload suspended 
+	// after a failed check (after it transitioned to False).
+	// After that the check state goes to "Unknown".
+	// The default is 15 min. 
+	RetryDelayMinutes *int64 `json:"retryDelayMinutes,omitempty"`
+
+	// A reference to the additional parameters for the check. 
+	Parameters *AdmissionCheckParametersReference `json:"parameters,omitempty"`
+
+	// How should the workload book quota (and possibly preempt others) 
+	// before the check pass. The default is NoBooking.
+	// If different modes are used for different AdmissionChecks,
+	// the most restrictive one is used.
+	QuotaBooking *QuotaBookingMode `json:"quotaBooking,omitempty"`
+}
+
+const (
+	// No booking, unless a check explicitely asks for it reporting quota exhausted.
+	NoBooking QuotaBookingMode = "NoBooking"
+	
+	// Book quota (and preempt) immediately after the basic quota checks 
+	// are done, without waiting for the additional checks to cpmplete.
+	BookAfterQuotaCheck QuotaBookingMode = "BookAfterQuotaCheck"
```

  > +1 on Marcin. The quota might be violated if we defer preemption.
  
  There should be a new check (managed the built in controller discussed offline) which, regardless to when the eviction is triggerd will be set to ready only after the necessary eviction process ended.

  But it has no indication that the quota is blocked.
